GALLANTRY   AWARDS
IT is hereby notified that H IS E XCELLENCY  THE P RESIDENT  of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka and
Commander-in-Chief of the Armed Forces has been graciously pleased to confer the Gallantry Awards of Parama Weera
Vibhushanaya, Weerodara Vibhushanaya, Weera Wickrema Vibhushanaya, Rana Wickrema Padakkama, Rana Sura Padakkama
on the 27th day of October in the Year Two Thousand Sixteen, to the persons named in the schedule hereto.
                                                              By His Excellency’s Command,
 
P. B. ABEYKOON,
Secretary to the President.
At the Presidential Secretariat,
Colombo,
19th August 2016.
The Parama Weera Vibhushanaya
Sri Lanka Army
Srl. No. Reg. No. Rank Name Regt
1 O/64556 Maj WMISB Walisundara RSP (Posthumous) GR
2 S/362939 Sgt Anura AM RSP (Posthumous) SLSR
3 S/371780 L/Cpl Rajapaksha KGM (Posthumous) SLSR
1A - G24359 – 57  (2016/10)
N.B.–  Sinhala and Tamil versions are published separately.
